    <dl>
           <dt>gha 1</dt>
           <dd><em>gha</em> the 4th consonant of the Sansk&#x1e5b;it alphabet (aspirate of the preceding)</dd>

           <dt>&#x22d9; ghak&#x0101;ra </dt>
           <dd><em>&#x25cb;k&#x0101;ra</em> m. the letter or sound <em>gha</em></dd>

           <dt>gha 2</dt>
           <dd><em>gha</em> ind. (used to lay stress on a word) at least, surely, verily, indeed, especially (= Gk. ?), [375, 1] <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#RV">RV.</a> <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#AV">AV.</a> v, 13, 10 &amp; 11 ; vi, 1, 3. In the Sa&#x1e43;hit&#x0101; the final vowel is generally lengthened (<em>gh&#x0101;</em>, <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#cf">cf.</a> P&#x0101;&#x1e47;. 6-3, 133) </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; as a rule it is preceded by other particles (<em>ut&#x00e1;</em>, <em>ut&#x00f3;</em>, <em>ut&#x00e1; v&#x0101;</em>, <em>cid</em>, <em>n&#x00e1;</em>, <em>v&#x0101;</em>) or by a pronoun or a preposition </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; it is also found between <em>iva</em> and <em>&#x00ed;d</em> </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; or between <em>iva</em> and <em>&#x00ed;d aha</em>, or between <em>v&#x0101;</em> and <em>&#x00ed;d</em> </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; sometimes it occurs in the clause which depends on a conditional or relative sentence (e.g. <em>&#x0101;&#x0341; gh&#x0101; gamad y&#x00e1;di &#x015b;r&#x00e1;vat</em>, 'he will surely come when he hears' <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#RV">RV.</a> i, 30, 8), i, 161, 8 ; viii, 46, 4</dd>

           <dt>gha 3</dt>
           <dd><em>gha</em> mfn. (&#x221a;<em>han</em>) ifc. 'striking, killing', cf. <em>j&#x012b;va-</em>, <em>t&#x0101;&#x1e0d;a-</em>, <em>p&#x0101;&#x1e47;i-</em>, <em>r&#x0101;ja-</em>, &amp;c. (cf. also <em>parigha</em>) </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; (<em>&#x0101;</em>), f. a stroke <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#L">L.</a></dd>

           <dt>gha 4</dt>
           <dd><em>gha</em> m. a rattling or gurgling or tinkling sound <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#L">L.</a> </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; a bell <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#L">L.</a> </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; (<em>&#x0101;</em>), f. a tinkling ornament worn by women round the waist</dd>

           <dt>gha&#x1e43;&#x1e63; </dt>
           <dd><em>gha&#x1e43;&#x1e63;</em> (and <em>gha&#x1e43;s</em>), cl. 1. &#x0100;. <em>&#x25cb;&#x1e63;ate</em> (and <em>&#x25cb;sate</em>), to diffuse lustre or splendour <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#Dh&#x0101;tup">Dh&#x0101;tup.</a> xvi, 50 </dd>
           <dd>&#x2022; to flow, stream <a href="worksAuthorsAbbrs.html#ib">ib.</a></dd>
